29.3(1): lha mo'i rjes su 'brang nas/ g.yung drung sems dpa'i spyod pa zab mos/ mchog thun 
29.4(1): dngos grub snyems par 'dod na/ sems can gang zhig blo ldan dag gis/ srod

29.12(1): thogs med stobs shugs stobs dang rab ldan/ phyi mar dga' ldan dag pa'i zhing

30.1(1): pha rol gyis rgol ba thams cad tshar bcad cing / dge ba'i stobs mchog rgya chen po

30.3(1): mar dge ba'i stobs mchog chen po'i mthu dpal gyis/ sgrib gnyis byang zhing tshogs

31.1(1): lta bu'i sgo nas bstod pa lags/ zhes gsol pas/ de la ston pas tshangs pa gtsug 
31.2(1): phud la/ yum chen mo thugs rje byams ma la bstod pa tshig bzhi tshigs su bcad pa 
31.3(1): 'di dag bka' bstsal to/ /A+o~M ma ba ma de ma hi mo ha e ma ho ma ye ru pa ye ta 'du 
31.4(1): 'du swahA: na mo dus gsum gyi bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum du gyur pa 
31.5(1): thugs rje byams ma la bstod pa/ phyag 'tshal byams ma chen mo brtse ma/ lha mo'i sku 
31.6(1): la thugs rje 'byung gnas/ 'gro kun skyabs mgon zhing du gyur cing / thugs rje bzhi 
31.7(1): ldan 'gro ba 'dren ma/ phyag 'tshal dbang ldan bkod pa'i zhing du/ bskal bzang 
31.8(1): sangs rgyas stong gi dbus na/ mtshan dpe yon tan lhun la rdzogs shing / longs 
31.9(1): spyod rdzogs pa'i sku ru bzhugs na/ phyag 'tshal sku mdog in+t+ra nI la/ dri ma med cing 
31.10(1): shel 'od 'bar bas/ 'khor ba'i chags skyon dri ma bral zhing / 'dam gyi pad mo'i 
31.11(1): tshul du gnas ma/ phyag 'tshal dbu gtsug lcang lor rdzogs sku/ ye shes lnga ldan lhun 
31.12(1): gyis grub pas/ rigs lnga'i dkyil 'khor dbu la rdzogs shing / gzhan snang 'khor 
31.13(1): ba zil gyis gnon ma/ phyag 'tshal zhal ras zla ba nya rgyas/ gzi mdangs 'od zer 
31.14(1): kun nas 'phro bas/ 'jig rten gsum gyi dga' ba bskyed cing / mgu ba chen po'i 
31.15(1): tshul dang ldan ma/ phyag 'tshal thugs rje tshad med spyan las/ kun gsal rig pa'i 
31.16(1): don dang ldan ma/ spyan drug yul drug rnam par gzigs shing / spyan gcig bsgribs 
31.17(1): med dbyings na gnas ma/ phyag 'tshal ye sangs ha lo snyan la/ kun gsan dngos 
31.18(1): med snyan dang ldan pas/ sna tshogs sgra yi bye brag 'byed cing / sgra tshogs ma lus

31.20(1): don dang ldan pas/ sna tshogs dri yi bye brag 'byed cing / dri rnams ma lus dbyings 
31.21(1): su gcod ma/ phyag 'tshal bon nyid ro len ljags la/ kun grol ye thim don dang 
32.1(1): ldan pas/ ro rnams ma lus dbyings su rol zhing / ro drug myong stong dbyings su

32.15(1): rje/ sa gzhi lta bu'i don dang ldan pas/ ci 'dod yid bzhin phun sum tshogs shing /

415.2(1): gshis/ 'dir bon gyi gzhung lugs ngo ma shes 'dod na bon gyi gsung rab dpe cha 'di 
415.3(1): lta bu la blta klog dang zhib 'jug gnang re'i ched dang / g.yung drung bon gyi bla sprul 
415.4(1): mkhas dbang mang pos yun ring re bskul byas pa'i rkyen dang / rgya che'i bod yig klog 
415.5(1): pa po yongs la blta bde 'khyer sla'i cha rkyen du dmigs nas/ ston pa'i gsung rab lung 
415.6(1): gi bon rin po che'i skor deb phreng brgya dang lnga bcu can zhig yig dkar gyi lam nas 
415.7(1): legs bsgrigs byas te/ rje smra seng bla ma'i gsung gi byin rlabs las 'phos pa/ g.yung 
415.8(1): drung bon gyi rgyud gzhung rin po che'i khrod kyi thun mong min pa'i brda chad/[ <<]gsung rab 
415.9(1): sgo mdzod rin po che'i glegs bam[>>]zhes pa dpe tshogs spyi chings kyi mtshan du gsol nas 
415.10(1): dpar 'grems zhus pa yin/
415.11(1): zhus dag thad las rim dngos la thog ma'i ma dpe gang la byas pa/ bar du dpe cha 
415.12(1): gang du bsdur ba/ bsdur ba'i legs cha gang zhig thon pa sogs glegs bam so so'i nang 
415.13(1): dang mjug gi zhus bsgrigs gsal bshad du bris yod/ mdor na nged las mi yongs 
415.14(1): kyis spyi lo 2011lo nas bzung mi lo lnga yi ring dad pa dag snang dang rang gi dge sbyor 
415.15(1): dang bstan la zhabs phyi gtso bzung thog deb rer tshar grangs bco lnga nas nyi shu bar 
415.16(1): zhus dag byas yod pas sngar las lhag pa'i legs cha zhig thon yod pa'i re ba yod/ 'on 
415.17(1): kyang re 'ga' ma dpe gcig ma gtogs bsdur ya ma rnyed pa dang / re 'ga' bsdur ya 
415.18(1): du ma rnyed kyang bris pa'i chad lhag sogs kyis gcig mtshungs med pa dang / nged zhus 
415.19(1): sgrig pa tsho'i mkhyen dpyod tshad brgal can min pa bcas dang rjes 'gro byas pas nor 
415.20(1): 'khrul gyis bslad pa'ang yod nges pas/ rjes gzigs mkhan rnam pas su dang gang la 
415.21(1): khag dkri med pa rang bstan rang skyong gi 'gan 'khri gtsang ma phrag tu khur ste bstan pa 
415.22(1): rin po che'i ched du nor 'khrul yo bsrang dag ther gnang ba'i skul ma zhu rgyu dang /
416.1(1): mthar don du nged [<<]g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang 
416.2(1): gis las don rlabs chen 'di 'dra zhig legs grub byung ba ni/ rig gzhung 'di dang 
416.3(1): bstan pa 'di la lhag bsam can gyis phyar gru mnyam 'degs byas pa las byung ba 
416.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
416.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
416.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
416.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
416.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
416.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
416.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
416.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
416.12(1):         7skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
416.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
416.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
416.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
416.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
416.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
416.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
416.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi 
416.20(1): ma 'gro kun yongs la shar ba'i smon 'dun dang bcas 'byung ldan 301 spyi lo 2015 5[ / ]1
